r4882 | wrtlprnft | 2006-06-14 00:29:45 +0200 (Wed, 14 Jun 2006) | 7 lines

Various little things.
- Added a new config item FORBID_COCKPIT_DATA, which can be used by the server to forbid certain data to be displayed on the client. It contains a colon (':') separated list of data sources to be disallowed
- Moved the definition of the map that contains the callback names and function pointers to cCockpit.cpp (was in cWidgetBase.cpp) and made it global (it doesn't get recreated and -sorted every time a new callback is parsed)
- Added the callback parameter to various config types in nNetwork, needed by FORBID_COCKPIT_DATA
- Re- added (must have forgot to commit last time) FONT_SIZE_FACTOR, a factor that is applied globally to every rendered font (defaults to 0.9)
- Re- added cCockpit.cpp to main_SOURCES in src/Makefile.am so it gets linked on the dedicated server

r4748 | davidfancella | 2006-06-04 12:12:22 +0200 (Sun, 04 Jun 2006) | 6 lines

Added SOUND_BUFFER_SIZE.  It's a float that gets multiplied by 512, the result is the number of samples in the sound buffer.  Default is 
0.5, which results in 256 samples in the buffer.  Should fix scratchy music playing during heavy load, and also make sound work for people 
for whom it doesn't work.

Also commented the now spurious gHud.h include in gMenus.cpp.  Do we need it?  The file is gone...

 ------------------------------------------------------------------------
 r4700 | z-man | 2006-06-02 19:53:16 +0200 (Fri, 02 Jun 2006) | 4 lines
 
 Restructuring of build process. Instead of one huge makefile that regenerates its includes and hopes all variables are up to date 
 (ensuring havoc if that is not the case, which often enough happens), a top level makefile recurses into four other makefiles, each
 one of them responsible for a set of includes generated by previous makefiles. The true work is now done in WorkMakefile.

r4631 | nemostultae | 2006-05-30 22:36:08 +0200 (Tue, 30 May 2006) | 29 lines

MacOS/Armagetron Advanced.tmproj: Updated. Building currently only works if you apply [this patch](http://lists.macromates.com/pipermail/textmate/2006-May/010751.html) to Xcode.bundle, but should work in a future version unmodified.

MacOS/Armagetron Advanced.xcodeproj/project.pbxproj:
  - srcdir may now be placed anywhere, manual intervention was required when it was anywhere else besides ~/.
  - Frameworks are now at /Library/Frameworks/ArmagetronAdvanced/{current, 10.2.8}.
  - Adapted headers search paths and framework search paths to reflect new framework location.
  - Added support for non-default build directory. Default is $srcdir/../armagetronad-build, and may be changed with the Xcode environment variable SYMROOT.
  - Adapted scripts to use MacOS/Rakefile.
  - Switched to gcc 4
  - Note: The Armagetron Advanced 10.2.8 and Armagetron Advanced Dedicated targets have not yet been updated.

MacOS/build: Xcode always generates this directory -- ignore it.

MacOS/build_tools: Removed. Succeeded by MacOS/Rakefile.

MacOS/Rakefile: Added. You must install [rake](http://rubyforge.org/projects/rake)

src/macosx/config_common.h.in: Added MACOSX_XCODE define, as some users may compile on Mac OS X using automake.

src/macosx/config_common.h: moved to src/macosx/config_common.h.in.

src/macosx/SDLMain.nib: Added.

src/tools/tDirectories.cpp:
  - (FindDataPath) changed ifndef to use MACOSX_XCODE.
  - (FindConfigurationPath) ditto.
  - (tDirectoriesCommandLineAnalyzer::DoInitialize) ditto.
  - (var s_topSourceDir) Unused variable if MACOSX_XCODE is defined
